2109</section>

2110<section id="_494">

2111<h3 id="_495" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2112Late effects that affect the brain and spinal cord may cause certain health problems.</h3>

2113<p id="_496" tabindex="-1">

2114Childhood cancer survivors who received radiation, certain types of chemotherapy, or surgery to the brain or spinal cord have an increased risk of late effects to the brain and spinal cord and related health problems. These include the following:

2115

2116 </p>

2117<div class="pdq-content-list">

2118<ul id="_497">

2119<li>

2120Headaches that may go away after <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=390324&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000390324&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2121vomiting</a>

2122.</li>

2123<li>

2124Loss of balance, lack of coordination, or trouble walking.</li>

2125<li>

2126Dizziness.</li>

2127<li>

2128Seizures.</li>

2129<li>

2130Loss of the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46276&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046276&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2131myelin</a>

2132 sheath that covers <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=373935&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000373935&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2133nerve</a>

2134 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46401&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046401&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2135fibers</a>

2136 in the brain.</li>

2137<li>

2138Movement <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=407758&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000407758&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2139disorders</a>

2140 that affect the legs and eyes or the ability to speak and swallow.</li>

2141<li>

2142Nerve damage in the hands or feet.</li>

2143<li>

2144Stroke. A second stroke may be more likely in survivors who received radiation to the brain, have a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=642021&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000642021&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2145history</a>

2146 of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=458091&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000458091&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2147high blood pressure</a>

2148, or were older than 40 years when they had their first stroke. </li>

2149<li>

2150Daytime sleepiness.</li>

2151<li>

2152<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45498&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045498&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2153Hydrocephalus</a>

2154.</li>

2155<li>

2156Loss of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46501&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046501&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2157bladder</a>

2158 and/or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46500&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046500&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2159bowel</a>

2160 control.</li>

2161<li>

2162Cavernomas (clusters of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44636&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044636&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2163abnormal</a>

2164 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45020&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045020&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2165blood vessels</a>

2166).</li>

2167<li>

2168Back pain.</li>

2169</ul>

2170</div>

2171<p id="_498" tabindex="-1">

2172Survivors may also have late effects that affect thinking, learning, memory, emotions, and behavior. </p>

2173<p id="_921" tabindex="-1">

2174New ways of using more targeted and lower <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44664&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044664&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2175doses</a>

2176 of radiation to the brain may lessen the risk of brain and spinal cord late effects.</p>

2177</section>

2178<section id="_574">

2179<h3 id="_575" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2180Possible signs and symptoms of brain and spinal cord late effects include headaches, loss of coordination, and seizures.</h3>

2181<p id="_576" tabindex="-1">

2182These <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2183signs</a>

2184 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2185symptoms</a>

2186 may be caused by brain and spinal cord late effects or by other <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2187conditions</a>

2188:

2189

2190</p>

2191<div class="pdq-content-list">

2192<ul id="_577">

2193<li>

2194Trouble speaking or swallowing.</li>

2195<li>

2196Trouble with having the eyes work together.</li>

2197<li>

2198Numbness, tingling, or weakness in the hands or feet.</li>

2199<li>

2200Being unable to bend the ankle to lift the foot up.</li>

2201<li>

2202Sudden numbness or weakness of the face, arm, or leg (especially on one side of the body).</li>

2203<li>

2204Unusual sleepiness or change in activity level.</li>

2205<li>

2206Unusual changes in personality or behavior.</li>

2207<li>

2208A change in bowel habits or trouble <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46642&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046642&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2209urinating</a>

2210.</li>

2211<li>

2212Increase in head size (in infants).

2213</li>

2214<li>

2215Sudden <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450096&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450096&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2216confusion</a>

2217 or trouble speaking or understanding speech.</li>

2218<li>

2219Sudden trouble seeing with one or both eyes.</li>

2220<li>

2221Sudden severe headache for no known reason.

2222</li>

2223</ul>

2224</div>

2225<p id="_578" tabindex="-1">

2226Other signs and symptoms include the following:</p>

2227<div class="pdq-content-list">

2228<ul id="_579">

2229<li>

2230Problems with memory.</li>

2231<li>

2232Problems with paying attention.</li>

2233<li>

2234Trouble with solving problems.</li>

2235<li>

2236Trouble with organizing thoughts and tasks.</li>

2237<li>

2238Slower ability to learn and use new information.</li>

2239<li>

2240Trouble learning to read, write, or do math.</li>

2241<li>

2242Trouble coordinating movement between the eyes, hands, and other muscles.</li>

2243<li>

2244Delays in normal <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450103&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450103&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2245development</a>

2246.</li>

2247<li>

2248Social withdrawal or trouble getting along with others.</li>

2249</ul>

2250</div>

2251<p id="_778" tabindex="-1">

2252Talk to your child's doctor if your child has any of these problems.</p>

2253</section>

2254<section id="_580">

2255<h3 id="_581" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2256Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the brain and spinal cord.</h3>

2257<p id="_1002" tabindex="-1">

2258In addition to asking about your child's personal and family <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2259health history</a>

2260 and doing a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2261physical exam</a>

2262, your child's doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

2263<div class="pdq-content-list">

2264<ul id="_583">

2265<li>

2266<strong>

2267<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=322871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000322871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2268Neurological exam</a>

2269</strong>

2270: A series of questions and tests to check the brain, spinal cord, and nerve function. The exam checks a person&#8217;s mental status, coordination, and ability to walk normally, and how well the muscles, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=792756&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000792756&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2271senses</a>

2272, and reflexes work. This may also be called a neuro exam or a neurologic exam.

2273In some cases, a more complete exam may be done by a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46267&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046267&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2274neurologist</a>

2275 or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46269&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046269&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2276neurosurgeon</a>

2277.</li>

2278<li>

2279<strong>

2280Neuropsychological <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=430407&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000430407&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2281assessment</a>

2282</strong>

2283: A series of tests to examine the patient's mental processes and behavior. Areas that are checked usually include:

2284

2285<div class="pdq-content-list">

2286<ul id="_584" class="list-dash">

2287<li>

2288Knowing who and where you are and what day it is.</li>

2289<li>

2290Ability to learn and remember new information. </li>

2291<li>

2292Intelligence.</li>

2293<li>

2294Ability to solve problems.</li>

2295<li>

2296Use of spoken and written language.</li>

2297<li>

2298Eye-hand coordination.</li>

2299<li>

2300Ability to organize information and tasks.</li>

2301</ul>

2302</div>

2303</li>

2304</ul>

2305</div>

2306<p id="_787" tabindex="-1">

2307Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of brain and spinal cord late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

2308

2309</p>

2310</section>

2311<section id="_507">

2312<h3 id="_508" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2313Survivors of childhood cancer may have anxiety and depression related to their cancer.</h3>

2314<p id="_509" tabindex="-1">

2315Survivors of childhood cancer may have <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=430405&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000430405&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2316anxiety</a>

2317 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=430479&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000430479&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2318depression</a>

2319 related to physical changes, having pain, the way they look, or the fear of cancer coming back. These and other factors may cause problems with personal relationships, education, employment, and health, and cause thoughts of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2320suicide</a>

2321. Survivors with these problems may be less likely to live on their own as adults.</p>

2322<p id="_868" tabindex="-1">

2323Follow-up exams for childhood cancer survivors should include <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46171&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046171&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2324screening</a>

2325 and treatment for possible <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=454766&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000454766&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2326psychological</a>

2327 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=454701&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000454701&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2328distress</a>

2329, such as anxiety, depression, and thoughts of suicide.</p>

2330<p id="_976" tabindex="-1">

2331For more information about psychological distress and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450097&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450097&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2332coping skills</a>

2333 for cancer patients, see the following <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44271&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044271&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2334PDQ</a>

2335 summaries:</p>

2336<div class="pdq-content-list">

2337<ul id="_999">

2338<li>

2339<a href="/about-cancer/coping/feelings/anxiety-distress-pdq">

2340Adjustment to Cancer: Anxiety and Distress</a>

2341</li>

2342<li>

2343<a href="/about-cancer/coping/feelings/depression-pdq">

2344Depression</a>

2345</li>

2346</ul>

2347</div>

2348</section>

2349<section id="_510">

2350<h3 id="_511" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2351Some childhood cancer survivors have post-traumatic stress disorder.</h3>

2352<p id="_512" tabindex="-1">

2353Being diagnosed and treated for a life-threatening disease may be traumatic. This <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=454807&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000454807&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2354trauma</a>

2355 may cause <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=440112&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000440112&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2356post-traumatic stress disorder</a>

2357 (PTSD). PTSD is defined as having certain behaviors following a stressful event that involved death or the threat of death, serious injury, or a threat to oneself or others. </p>

2358<p id="_514" tabindex="-1">

2359PTSD can affect cancer survivors in the following ways:</p>

2360<div class="pdq-content-list">

2361<ul id="_515">

2362<li>

2363Reliving the time they were diagnosed and treated for cancer, in nightmares or flashbacks, and thinking about it all the time.

2364</li>

2365<li>

2366Avoiding places, events, and people that remind them of the cancer experience. </li>

2367</ul>

2368</div>

2369<p id="_513" tabindex="-1">

2370In general, childhood cancer survivors show low levels of PTSD, depending in part on the coping style of patients and their parents. Survivors who received <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44971&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044971&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2371radiation therapy</a>

2372 to the head when younger than 4 years or survivors who received intensive treatment may be at higher risk of PTSD. Family problems, little or no <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=440116&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000440116&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2373social support</a>

2374 from family or friends, and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450122&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450122&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2375stress</a>

2376 not related to the cancer may increase the chances of having PTSD. </p>

2377<p id="_516" tabindex="-1">

2378Because avoiding places and persons connected to the cancer may be part of PTSD, survivors with PTSD may not get the medical treatment they need.</p>

2379</section>

2380<section id="_844">

2381<h3 id="_845" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2382Adolescents who are diagnosed with cancer may have social problems later in life.</h3>

2383<p id="_846" tabindex="-1">

2384<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=776825&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000776825&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2385Adolescents</a>

2386 who are diagnosed with cancer may reach fewer social milestones or reach them later in life than adolescents not diagnosed with cancer. Social milestones include having a first boyfriend or girlfriend, getting married, and having a child. They may also have trouble getting along with other people or feel like they are not liked by others their age.</p>

2387<p id="_869" tabindex="-1">

2388 Cancer survivors in this age group have reported being less satisfied with their health and their lives in general compared with others of the same age who did not have cancer. Adolescents and young adults who survived cancer need special programs that give psychological, educational, and job support.</p>

2389</section>

2390</div>

2391

2392 </section>

2395

2396 <section id="_152">

2397

2398 <h2>

2399Digestive System</h2>

2400

2401 <div id="_section_152" class="pdq-sections">

2402<div class="key-points">

2403<h3 id="_152_kpBoxHdr" do-not-show="toc">

2404Key Points</h3>

2405<div id="_kp_section_152_5">

2406<ul>

2407<li>

2408Teeth and jaws<ul>

2409<li>

2410Problems with the teeth and jaws are late effects that are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

2411<li>

2412Radiation to the head and neck and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of late effects to the teeth and jaws.</li>

2413<li>

2414Late effects that affect the teeth and jaws may cause certain health problems.</li>

2415<li>

2416Possible signs and symptoms of late effects of the teeth and jaws include tooth decay (cavities) and jaw pain.</li>

2417<li>

2418Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the mouth and jaws.</li>

2419<li>

2420Regular dental care is very important for survivors of childhood cancer.</li>

2421</ul>

2422</li>

2423<li>

2424Digestive tract<ul>

2425<li>

2426Digestive tract late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

2427<li>

2428Radiation to the bladder, prostate, or testicles and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of digestive tract late effects.</li>

2429<li>

2430Late effects that affect the digestive tract may cause certain health problems.</li>

2431<li>

2432Possible signs and symptoms of digestive tract late effects include abdominal pain and diarrhea.</li>

2433<li>

2434Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the digestive tract.</li>

2435</ul>

2436</li>

2437<li>

2438Liver and bile ducts<ul>

2439<li>

2440Liver and bile duct late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

2441<li>

2442Certain types of chemotherapy and radiation to the liver or bile ducts increase the risk of late effects.</li>

2443<li>

2444Late effects that affect the liver and bile ducts may cause certain health problems.

2445</li>

2446<li>

2447Possible signs and symptoms of liver and bile duct late effects include abdominal pain and jaundice.</li>

2448<li>

2449Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the liver and bile duct.</li>

2450<li>

2451Health habits that promote a healthy liver are important for survivors of childhood cancer. </li>

2452</ul>

2453</li>

2454<li>

2455Pancreas<ul>

2456<li>

2457Radiation therapy increases the risk of pancreatic late effects.</li>

2458<li>

2459Late effects that affect the pancreas may cause certain health problems.</li>

2460<li>

2461Possible signs and symptoms of pancreatic late effects include frequent urination and being thirsty.</li>

2462<li>

2463Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the pancreas.</li>

2464</ul>

2465</li>

2466</ul>

2467</div>

2468</div>

2588<section id="_599">

2589<h4 id="_600" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2590Possible signs and symptoms of late effects of the teeth and jaws include tooth decay (cavities) and jaw pain.</h4>

2591<p id="_601" tabindex="-1">

2592These and other <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2593signs</a>

2594 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2595symptoms</a>

2596 may be caused by late effects of the teeth and jaws or by other <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2597conditions</a>

2598:</p>

2599<div class="pdq-content-list">

2600<ul id="_602">

2601<li>

2602Teeth are small or do not have a normal shape.</li>

2603<li>

2604Missing permanent teeth.</li>

2605<li>

2606Permanent teeth come in at a later than normal age.</li>

2607<li>

2608Teeth have less enamel than normal.</li>

2609<li>

2610More tooth decay (cavities) and gum disease than normal.</li>

2611<li>

2612Dry mouth.</li>

2613<li>

2614Trouble chewing, swallowing, and speaking.</li>

2615<li>

2616Jaw pain.</li>

2617<li>

2618Jaws do not open and close the way they should.</li>

2619</ul>

2620</div>

2621<p id="_779" tabindex="-1">

2622Talk to your child's doctor if your child has any of these problems.</p>

2623</section>

2624<section id="_592">

2625<h4 id="_593" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2626Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the mouth and jaws.</h4>

2627<p id="_1003" tabindex="-1">

2628In addition to asking about your child's personal and family <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2629health history</a>

2630 and doing a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2631physical exam</a>

2632, your child's doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

2633<div class="pdq-content-list">

2634<ul id="_595">

2635<li>

2636<strong>

2637Dental exam</strong>

2638: An exam of the teeth, mouth, and jaws to check general signs of dental health, including checking for signs of disease, such as cavities or anything that seems unusual.This may also be called a dental check-up.</li>

2639<li>

2640<strong>

2641Panorex <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45944&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045944&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2642x-ray</a>

2643</strong>

2644: An x-ray of all of the teeth and their roots. An x-ray is a type of energy beam that can go through the body and onto film, making a picture of areas inside the body.</li>

2645<li>

2646<strong>

2647X-ray of the jaws</strong>

2648: An x-ray of the jaws. An x-ray is a type of energy beam that can go through the body and onto film, making a picture of areas inside the body.</li>

2649<li>

2650<strong>

2651<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46033&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046033&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2652CT scan</a>

2653 (CAT scan)</strong>

2654: A procedure that makes a series of detailed pictures of areas inside the body, such as the head and neck, taken from different angles. The pictures are made by a computer linked to an x-ray machine. This procedure is also called computed tomography, computerized tomography, or computerized axial tomography.</li>

2655<li>

2656<strong>

2657<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45788&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045788&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2658MRI</a>

2659 (magnetic resonance imaging)</strong>

2660: A procedure that uses a magnet, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=651209&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000651209&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2661radio waves</a>

2662, and a computer to make a series of detailed pictures of areas inside the body, such as the head and neck. This procedure is also called nuclear magnetic resonance imaging (NMRI). </li>

2663<li>

2664<strong>

2665<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45164&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045164&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2666Biopsy</a>

2667</strong>

2668: The removal of bone cells from the jaw so they can be viewed under a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=638184&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000638184&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2669microscope</a>

2670 to check for signs of bone death after radiation therapy.</li>

2671</ul>

2672</div>

2673<p id="_788" tabindex="-1">

2674Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of teeth and jaw late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

2675

2676</p>

2677</section>

2678<section id="_596">

2679<h4 id="_597" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2680Regular dental care is very important for survivors of childhood cancer.</h4>

2681<p id="_598" tabindex="-1">

2682Doctors suggest that survivors of childhood cancer have a dental check-up and a cleaning and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44670&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044670&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2683fluoride</a>

2684 treatment every 6 months. Children who had radiation therapy to the oral cavity may also see an <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=793501&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000793501&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2685orthodontist</a>

2686 or an <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46252&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046252&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2687otolaryngologist</a>

2688. If <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46324&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046324&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2689lesions</a>

2690 are present in the mouth, a biopsy may be needed.</p>

2737prostate</a>

2740.</li>

2748<section id="_607">

2749<h4 id="_608" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2750Radiation to the bladder, prostate, or testicles and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of digestive tract late effects.</h4>

2751<p id="_609" tabindex="-1">

2752The risk of health problems that affect the digestive tract increases after treatment with the following:</p>

2753<div class="pdq-content-list">

2754<ul id="_610">

2755<li>

2756Radiation therapy to the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45070&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045070&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2757abdomen</a>

2758 or areas near the abdomen, such as the esophagus, bladder, prostate, or testicles, may cause digestive tract problems that begin quickly and last for a short time. In some patients, however, digestive tract problems are delayed and long-lasting. These late effects are caused by radiation therapy that damages the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45020&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045020&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2759blood vessels</a>

2760. Receiving higher doses of radiation therapy or receiving chemotherapy such as <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45237&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045237&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2761dactinomycin</a>

2762 or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44916&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044916&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2763anthracyclines</a>

2764 together with radiation therapy may increase this risk.</li>

2765<li>

2766<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46684&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046684&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2767Abdominal</a>

2768 surgery or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45087&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045087&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2769pelvic</a>

2770 surgery to remove the bladder.</li>

2771<li>

2772Chemotherapy with alkylating agents such as cyclophosphamide, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=635746&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000635746&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2773procarbazine</a>

2779daunorubicin</a>

2780, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45254&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045254&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2887<section id="_615">

2888<h4 id="_616" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2889Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the digestive tract.</h4>

2890<p id="_1004" tabindex="-1">

2891In addition to asking about your child's personal and family health history and doing a physical exam, your child's doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

2892<div class="pdq-content-list">

2893<ul id="_618">

2894<li>

2895<strong>

2896<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45668&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045668&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2897Digital rectal exam</a>

2898</strong>

2899: An exam of the rectum. The doctor or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=269445&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000269445&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2900nurse</a>

2901 inserts a lubricated, gloved finger into the rectum to feel for lumps or anything else that seems unusual.

2902</li>

2903<li>

2904<strong>

2905<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=304685&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000304685&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2906Blood chemistry studies</a>

2907</strong>

2908: A procedure in which a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270735&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270735&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2909blood</a>

2910 sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain substances released into the blood by <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=257523&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000257523&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2911organs</a>

2912 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46683&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046683&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2913tissues</a>

2914 in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance can be a sign of disease.</li>

2915<li>

2916<strong>

2917<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46325&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046325&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2918Kidney</a>

2919, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46638&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046638&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2920ureter</a>

2921, and bladder <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45944&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045944&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2922x-ray</a>

2923</strong>

2924: An x-ray is a type of energy beam that can go through the body and onto film, making a picture of areas inside the body. An x-ray may be taken of the abdomen, kidney, ureter, or bladder to check for signs of disease.</li>

2925</ul>

2926</div>

2927<p id="_789" tabindex="-1">

2928Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of digestive tract late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

2964<section id="_623">

2965<h4 id="_624" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

2966Certain types of chemotherapy and radiation to the liver or bile ducts increase the risk of late effects.</h4>

2967<p id="_625" tabindex="-1">

2968The risk of liver or bile duct late effects may be increased in childhood cancer survivors treated with one of the following:</p>

2969<div class="pdq-content-list">

2970<ul id="_626">

2971<li>

2972Surgery to remove part of the liver or a liver <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46631&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046631&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2973transplant</a>

2974.</li>

2975<li>

2976Chemotherapy that includes high-dose cyclophosphamide as part of a stem cell transplant.</li>

2977<li>

2978Chemotherapy such as <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46639&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046639&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

29796-mercaptopurine</a>

2980, 6-<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46765&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046765&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2981thioguanine</a>

2982, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45393&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045393&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

2983methotrexate</a>

2984, and dactinomycin.</li>

2985<li>

2986Radiation therapy to the liver and bile ducts. The risk depends on the following:<div class="pdq-content-list">

2987<ul id="_627" class="list-dash">

2988<li>

2989The dose of radiation and how much of the liver is treated.</li>

2990<li>

2991Age when treated (the younger the age, the higher the risk).</li>

2992<li>

2993Whether there was surgery to remove part of the liver.</li>

2994<li>

2995Whether chemotherapy, such as doxorubicin or dactinomycin, was given together with radiation therapy.</li>

2996</ul>

2997</div>

2998</li>

2999<li>

3000Stem cell transplant.</li>

3001</ul>

3002</div>

3003<p id="_978" tabindex="-1">

3004The following may also increase the risk of liver and bile duct late effects:</p>

3009Hepatitis B</a>

3010 or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44139&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044139&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3013infection</a>

3014.</li>

3015<li>

3016History of chronic graft-versus-host disease.</li>

3017<li>

3018Liver damage caused by <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44806&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044806&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3019veno-occlusive disease</a>

3020/<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=723872&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000723872&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3021sinusoidal obstruction syndrome</a>

3022.</li>

3023<li>

3024Tissue and organ damage from the buildup of extra <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=446805&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000446805&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3025iron</a>

3026 after having many <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45991&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045991&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3027blood transfusions</a>

3032<section id="_184">

3033<h4 id="_185" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3034Late effects that affect the liver and bile ducts may cause certain health problems.

3035</h4>

3036<p id="_186" tabindex="-1">

3037Liver and bile duct late effects and related health problems include the following:</p>

3038<div class="pdq-content-list">

3039<ul id="_187">

3040<li>

3041Liver doesn&#8217;t work the way it should or stops working.</li>

3042<li>

3043<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=322135&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000322135&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3044Gallstones</a>

3045.</li>

3046<li>

3047<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45614&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045614&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3048Benign</a>

3049 liver lesions.</li>

3050<li>

3051Liver <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45690&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045690&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3052fibrosis</a>

3053 (an overgrowth of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44013&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044013&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3054connective tissue</a>

3055 in the liver) or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45478&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045478&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3058<li>

3065<section id="_629">

3066<h4 id="_630" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3067Possible signs and symptoms of liver and bile duct late effects include abdominal pain and jaundice.</h4>

3068<p id="_631" tabindex="-1">

3069 These and other signs and symptoms may be caused by liver and bile duct late effects or by other conditions:

3070

3071</p>

3072<div class="pdq-content-list">

3073<ul id="_632">

3074<li>

3075Weight gain or weight loss.</li>

3076<li>

3077Swelling of the abdomen.</li>

3078<li>

3079Nausea and vomiting.</li>

3080<li>

3081Pain in the abdomen. Pain may occur near the ribs, often on the right side, or after eating a fatty meal.</li>

3082<li>

3083<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46328&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046328&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3084Jaundice</a>

3085 (yellowing of the skin and whites of the eyes).

3086</li>

3087<li>

3088Light-colored bowel movements.</li>

3089<li>

3090Diarrhea.</li>

3091<li>

3092Dark-colored <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46642&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046642&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3093urine</a>

3094.</li>

3095<li>

3096A lot of gas.</li>

3097<li>

3098Lack of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=454699&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000454699&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3100.</li>

3101<li>

3102Feeling tired or weak.</li>

3103</ul>

3104</div>

3105<p id="_781" tabindex="-1">

3107<p id="_934" tabindex="-1">

3110<section id="_633">

3111<h4 id="_634" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3112Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the liver and bile duct.</h4>

3113<p id="_1005" tabindex="-1">

3114In addition to asking about your child's personal and family health history and doing a physical exam, your child's doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

3115<div class="pdq-content-list">

3116<ul id="_636">

3117<li>

3118<strong>

3119Blood chemistry studies</strong>

3120: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain substances released into the blood by organs and tissues in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance can be a sign of disease For example, there may be a higher level of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44518&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044518&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3121bilirubin</a>

3122, alanine aminotransferase (ALT), and aspartate aminotransferase (AST) in the body if the liver has been damaged.</li>

3123<li>

3124<strong>

3125<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=687214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000687214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3126Ferritin</a>

3127 level</strong>

3128: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amount of ferritin. Ferritin is a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46092&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046092&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3129protein</a>

3130 that binds to iron and stores it for use by the body. After a stem cell transplant, a high ferritin level may be a sign of liver disease.</li>

3131<li>

3132<strong>

3133<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45107&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045107&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3134Complete blood count</a>

3135 (CBC)</strong>

3136: A test in which a sample of blood is drawn and checked for the following:<div class="pdq-content-list">

3137<ul id="_980">

3138<li>

3139The number of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3140red blood cells</a>

3141, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45993&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045993&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3142white blood cells</a>

3143, and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45840&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045840&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3144platelets</a>

3145.</li>

3146<li>

3147The amount of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45108&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045108&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3148hemoglobin</a>

3149 (the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46092&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046092&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3150protein</a>

3151 that carries <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=538149&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000538149&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3152oxygen</a>

3153) in the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3154red blood cells</a>

3155.</li>

3156<li>

3157The portion of the blood sample made up of red blood cells.</li>

3158</ul>

3159</div>

3160<p id="_981" tabindex="-1">

3161This test is used to check the amount of platelets in the body.</p>

3162</li>

3163<li>

3164<strong>

3165Prothrombin time (PT) test</strong>

3166: A test that measures how long it takes for the blood to <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=476017&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000476017&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3167clot</a>

3168.</li>

3169<li>

3170<strong>

3171<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46371&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046371&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3172Hepatitis</a>

3173 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44528&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044528&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3174assay</a>

3175</strong>

3176: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked for pieces of the hepatitis <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45941&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045941&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3177virus</a>

3178. The blood sample may also be used to measure how much hepatitis virus is in the blood. All patients who had a blood transfusion before 1972 should have a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46171&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046171&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3179screening</a>

3180 test for hepatitis B. Patients who had a blood transfusion before 1993 should have a screening test for hepatitis C.</li>

3181<li>

3182<strong>

3183<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46157&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046157&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3184Ultrasound</a>

3185 exam</strong>

3186: A procedure in which high-energy sound waves (ultrasound) are bounced off internal tissues or organs, such as the gall bladder, and make echoes. The echoes form a picture of body tissues called a sonogram. The picture can be printed to be looked at later.

3187</li>

3188</ul>

3189</div>

3190<p id="_790" tabindex="-1">

3191Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of liver or bile duct late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

3192

3193</p>

3194</section>

3237<section id="_897">

3238<h4 id="_905" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3239Late effects that affect the pancreas may cause certain health problems.</h4>

3240<p id="_912" tabindex="-1">

3241Pancreatic late effects and related health problems include the following:</p>

3242<div class="pdq-content-list">

3243<ul id="_898">

3244<li>

3245<strong>

3246Insulin resistance</strong>

3247: A condition in which the body does not use insulin the way it should. Insulin is needed to help control the amount of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44033&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044033&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3248glucose</a>

3249 (a type of sugar) in the body. Because the insulin does not work the way it should, glucose and fat levels rise.</li>

3250<li>

3251<strong>

3252<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44129&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044129&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3253Diabetes mellitus</a>

3254</strong>

3255: A disease in which the body does not make enough insulin or does not use it the way it should. When there is not enough insulin, the amount of glucose in the blood increases and the kidneys make a large amount of urine.</li>

3256</ul>

3257</div>

3258</section>

3259<section id="_899">

3269Frequent urination.</li>

3273Feeling very hungry.</li>

3274<li>

3275Weight loss for no known reason.</li>

3276<li>

3277Feeling very tired.</li>

3278<li>

3279Frequent infections, especially of the skin, gums, or bladder.</li>

3280<li>

3281Blurred vision.</li>

3291<section id="_900">

3292<h4 id="_907" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3293Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the pancreas.</h4>

3294<p id="_1006" tabindex="-1">

3295In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family health history and doing a physical exam, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

3296<div class="pdq-content-list">

3297<ul id="_917">

3298<li>

3299<strong>

3300Glycated <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45108&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045108&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3301hemoglobin</a>

3302 (A1C) test</strong>

3303: A procedure in which a sample of blood is drawn and the amount of glucose that is attached to <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3304red blood cells</a>

3305 is measured. A higher-than-normal amount of glucose attached to red blood cells can be a sign of diabetes mellitus. </li>

3306<li>

3307<strong>

3308Fasting blood sugar test</strong>

3309: A test in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amount of glucose in the blood. This test is done after the patient has had nothing to eat overnight. A higher than normal amount of glucose in the blood can be a sign of diabetes mellitus. </li>

3310</ul>

3311</div>

3320 <section id="_198">

3321

3322 <h2>

3323Endocrine System</h2>

3324

3325 <div id="_section_198" class="pdq-sections">

3326<div class="key-points">

3327<h3 id="_198_kpBoxHdr" do-not-show="toc">

3328Key Points</h3>

3329<div id="_kp_section_198_6">

3330<ul>

3331<li>

3332Thyroid gland<ul>

3333<li>

3334Thyroid late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

3335<li>

3336Radiation therapy to the head and neck increases the risk of thyroid late effects. </li>

3337<li>

3338Late effects that affect the thyroid may cause certain health problems.</li>

3339<li>

3340Signs and symptoms of thyroid late effects depend on whether there is too little or too much thyroid hormone in the body.</li>

3341<li>

3342Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the thyroid.</li>

3343</ul>

3344</li>

3345<li>

3346Hypothalamus and pituitary gland<ul>

3347<li>

3348Neuroendocrine late effects may be caused after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

3349<li>

3350Treatment that affects the hypothalamus or pituitary gland increases the risk of neuroendocrine system late effects.

3351</li>

3352<li>

3353Late effects that affect the hypothalamus may cause certain health problems.</li>

3354<li>

3355Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the neuroendocrine system.</li>

3356</ul>

3357</li>

3358<li>

3359Testicles and ovaries</li>

3360<li>

3361Metabolic syndrome<ul>

3362<li>

3363Metabolic syndrome is more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

3364<li>

3365Radiation therapy increases the risk of metabolic syndrome.</li>

3366<li>

3367Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose metabolic syndrome.</li>

3368<li>

3369Metabolic syndrome may cause heart and blood vessel disease and diabetes.</li>

3370</ul>

3371</li>

3372<li>

3373Weight<ul>

3374<li>

3375Being underweight, being overweight, or having obesity is a late effect that is more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.

3376

3377</li>

3378<li>

3379Radiation therapy increases the risk of being underweight, being overweight, or having obesity.</li>

3380<li>

3381Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose a change in weight.</li>

3382</ul>

3383</li>

3384</ul>

3385</div>

3386</div>

3387<section id="_870">

3388<h3 id="_871" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3389Thyroid gland</h3>

3390<section id="_642">

3391<h4 id="_643" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3392Thyroid late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</h4>

3393<p id="_644" tabindex="-1">

3477<h4 id="_199" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3478Late effects that affect the thyroid may cause certain health problems.</h4>

3479<p id="_200" tabindex="-1">

3480Thyroid late effects and related health problems include the following:</p>

3481<div class="pdq-content-list">

3482<ul id="_201">

3483<li>

3484<strong>

3485<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44547&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044547&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3486Hypothyroidism</a>

3487 (not enough <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44558&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044558&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3488thyroid hormone</a>

3489)</strong>

3490: There is a higher risk of hypothyroidism in survivors treated with head and neck radiation involving the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44751&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044751&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3491thyroid gland</a>

3492, especially survivors of Hodgkin lymphoma. This is the most common thyroid late effect. It usually occurs 2 to 5 years after treatment ends but may occur longer than 25 years after radiation therapy. It is more common in girls than boys.</li>

3493<li>

3494<strong>

3495<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45717&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045717&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3496Hyperthyroidism</a>

3497 (too much thyroid hormone)</strong>

3498: The risk of hyperthyroidism increases with higher doses of radiation therapy to the thyroid gland. Hyperthyroidism is less common than hypothyroidism. It usually occurs 5 years after treatment ends, but may occur longer than 25 years after radiation therapy. </li>

3499<li>

3500<strong>

3501<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44545&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044545&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3502Goiter</a>

3503</strong>

3504 (an enlarged thyroid).</li>

3505<li>

3506<strong>

3507Lumps in the thyroid</strong>

3508: Higher radiation dose and longer time since diagnosis are linked to an increased risk of developing thyroid lumps. These growths may be <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45614&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045614&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3509benign</a>

3510 (not cancerous) or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45772&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045772&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3511malignant</a>

3512 (cancer). It is more common in girls than boys. </li>

3513</ul>

3603<section id="_656">

3604<h4 id="_657" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3605Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the thyroid.</h4>

3606<p id="_1007" tabindex="-1">

3607In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3608health history</a>

3609 and doing a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3610physical exam</a>

3611, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

3612<div class="pdq-content-list">

3613<ul id="_659">

3614<li>

3615<strong>

3616<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270735&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270735&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3617Blood</a>

3618 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45713&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045713&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3619hormone</a>

3620 studies</strong>

3621: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain hormones released into the blood by <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=257523&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000257523&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3622organs</a>

3623 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46683&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046683&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3624tissues</a>

3625 in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance can be a sign of disease in the organ or tissue that makes it. The blood may be checked for <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44636&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044636&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3626abnormal</a>

3627 levels of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44559&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044559&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3628thyroid-stimulating hormone</a>

3629 (TSH) or free <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=533434&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000533434&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3630thyroxine</a>

3631 (T4). </li>

3632<li>

3633<strong>

3634<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46157&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046157&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3635Ultrasound</a>

3636 exam</strong>

3637: A procedure in which high-energy sound waves (ultrasound) are bounced off internal tissues or organs and make echoes. The echoes form a picture of body tissues called a sonogram. The picture can be printed to be looked at later. This procedure can show the size of the thyroid and whether there are <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44502&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044502&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3638nodules</a>

3639 (lumps) on the thyroid.</li>

3640</ul>

3641</div>

3642<p id="_791" tabindex="-1">

3643Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of thyroid late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.
