3649<h3 id="_890" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3650Hypothalamus and pituitary gland</h3>

3651<section id="_441">

3652<h4 id="_442" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3653Neuroendocrine late effects may be caused after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</h4>

3654<p id="_443" tabindex="-1">

3655The <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45803&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045803&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3656neuroendocrine</a>

3657 system is the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=446114&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000446114&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3658nervous system</a>

3659 and the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=468796&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000468796&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3660endocrine system</a>

3661 working together. </p>

3662<p id="_925" tabindex="-1">

3663Treatment for these and other childhood cancers may cause neuroendocrine late effects:</p>

3664<div class="pdq-content-list">

3665<ul id="_444">

3666<li>

3667<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45586&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045586&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3668Acute lymphoblastic leukemia</a>

3669 (ALL).</li>

3670<li>

3671<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45645&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045645&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3672Brain and spinal cord tumors</a>

3673.

3674</li>

3675<li>

3676Cancers treated with total-body irradiation (TBI) before a stem cell transplant.</li>

3677</ul>

3678</div>

3679</section>

3680<section id="_431">

3681<h4 id="_432" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3682Treatment that affects the hypothalamus or pituitary gland increases the risk of neuroendocrine system late effects.

3683</h4>

3684<p id="_445" tabindex="-1">

3685Childhood cancer survivors have an increased risk for neuroendocrine late effects. These effects are caused by radiation therapy to the brain in the area of the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46359&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046359&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3686hypothalamus</a>

3687. The hypothalamus controls the way hormones are made and released into the bloodstream by the pituitary gland. Radiation therapy may be given to treat cancer near the hypothalamus or as total-body irradiation before a stem cell transplant. These effects are also caused by <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45570&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045570&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3688surgery</a>

3689 in the area of the hypothalamus, pituitary gland, or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=637726&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000637726&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3690optic pathways</a>

3691.</p>

3692<p id="_532" tabindex="-1">

3693Childhood cancer survivors who have neuroendocrine late effects may have low levels of any of the following hormones made in the pituitary gland and released into the blood:</p>

3694<div class="pdq-content-list">

3695<ul id="_446">

3696<li>

3697<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=538639&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000538639&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3698Growth hormone</a>

3699 (helps promote growth and control <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46173&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046173&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3700metabolism</a>

3701).</li>

3702<li>

3703<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=476632&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000476632&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3704Adrenocorticotropic hormone</a>

3705 (ACTH; controls the making of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45295&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045295&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3706glucocorticoids</a>

3707).</li>

3708<li>

3709<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=476644&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000476644&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3710Prolactin</a>

3711 (controls the making of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=304766&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000304766&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3712breast</a>

3713 milk).</li>

3714<li>

3715<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44559&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044559&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3716Thyroid-stimulating hormone</a>

3717 (TSH; controls the making of thyroid hormones).</li>

3718<li>

3719<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=643019&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000643019&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3720Luteinizing hormone</a>

3721 (LH; controls reproduction).</li>

3722<li>

3723<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=643012&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000643012&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3724Follicle-stimulating hormone</a>

3725 (FSH; controls reproduction).</li>

3726</ul>

3727</div>

3728</section>

3729<section id="_720">

3730<h4 id="_721" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3731Late effects that affect the hypothalamus may cause certain health problems.</h4>

3732<p id="_722" tabindex="-1">

3733Neuroendocrine late effects and related health problems include the following:

3734

3735</p>

3736<div class="pdq-content-list">

3737<ul id="_723">

3738<li>

3739<strong>

3740Growth hormone <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=321364&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000321364&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3741deficiency</a>

3742</strong>

3743: A low level of growth hormone is a common late effect of radiation to the brain in childhood cancer survivors. The higher the radiation dose and the longer the time since treatment, the greater the risk of this late effect. A low level of growth hormone may also occur in childhood ALL and stem cell transplant survivors who received radiation therapy to the brain and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=340937&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000340937&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3744spinal cord</a>

3745 and/or chemotherapy. <p id="_926" tabindex="-1">

3746A low level of growth hormone in childhood results in adult height that is shorter than normal. If the child's bones have not fully developed, low growth hormone levels may be treated with growth <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46127&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046127&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3747hormone replacement therapy</a>

3748 beginning one year after the end of treatment.</p>

3749</li>

3750<li>

3751<strong>

3752Adrenocorticotropin deficiency</strong>

3753: A low level of adrenocorticotropic hormone is an uncommon late effect. It may occur in childhood brain tumor survivors, survivors with low growth hormone levels or central hypothyroidism, or after radiation therapy to the brain. <p id="_927" tabindex="-1">

3754Symptoms of deficiency may not be severe and may not be noticed. Signs and symptoms of adrenocorticotropin deficiency include the following: </p>

3755<div class="pdq-content-list">

3756<ul id="_928" class="list-dash">

3757<li>

3758Weight loss for no known reason.</li>

3759<li>

3760Not feeling hungry.</li>

3761<li>

3762<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=390302&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000390302&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3763Nausea</a>

3764.</li>

3765<li>

3766<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=390324&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000390324&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3767Vomiting</a>

3768.</li>

3769<li>

3770<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46684&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046684&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3771Abdominal</a>

3772 pain.</li>

3773<li>

3774Low <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=462668&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000462668&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3775blood pressure</a>

3776.</li>

3777<li>

3778Feeling tired.</li>

3779<li>

3780Dizziness.</li>

3781</ul>

3782</div>

3783<p id="_929" tabindex="-1">

3784Low levels of adrenocorticotropin may be treated with <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45205&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045205&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3785hydrocortisone</a>

3786 therapy.</p>

3787</li>

3788<li>

3789<strong>

3790Hyperprolactinemia</strong>

3791: A high level of the hormone prolactin may occur after a high dose of radiation to the brain or surgery that affects part of the pituitary gland. A high level of prolactin may cause the following:<div class="pdq-content-list">

3792<ul id="_922" class="list-dash">

3793<li>

3794<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=440113&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000440113&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3795Puberty</a>

3796 at a later age than normal.</li>

3797<li>

3798Flow of breast milk in a woman who is not pregnant or breast-feeding.</li>

3799<li>

3800Less frequent or no menstrual periods or menstrual periods with a very light flow.</li>

3801<li>

3802<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=256567&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000256567&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3803Hot flashes</a>

3804.</li>

3805<li>

3806Inability to become pregnant.</li>

3807<li>

3808Inability to have an <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=373933&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000373933&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3809erection</a>

3810 needed for sexual intercourse.</li>

3811<li>

3812Lower <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=651212&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000651212&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3813sex drive</a>

3814 (in men and women).</li>

3815<li>

3816<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=538637&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000538637&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3817Osteopenia</a>

3818 (low bone mineral density).</li>

3819</ul>

3820</div>

3821<p id="_930" tabindex="-1">

3822Sometimes there are no signs and symptoms. Treatment is rarely needed.</p>

3823</li>

3824<li>

3825<strong>

3826<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44559&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044559&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3827Thyroid-stimulating hormone</a>

3828 deficiency</strong>

3829 (central hypothyroidism): A low level of thyroid hormone may occur very slowly over time after radiation therapy to the brain. <p id="_931" tabindex="-1">

3830Sometimes the symptoms of thyroid-stimulating hormone deficiency are not noticed. Low thyroid hormone levels may cause slow growth and delayed puberty, as well as <a href="/types/childhood-cancers/late-effects-pdq#_651">

3831other symptoms</a>

3832. A low level of thyroid hormone may be treated with <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=563955&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000563955&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3833thyroid hormone replacement therapy</a>

3834.</p>

3835</li>

3836<li>

3837<strong>

3838Luteinizing hormone or follicle-stimulating hormone deficiency</strong>

3839: Low levels of these hormones can cause different health problems. The type of problem depends on the radiation dose. <p id="_932" tabindex="-1">

3840Childhood cancer survivors who were treated with lower doses of radiation to the brain may develop central precocious puberty (a condition that causes puberty to start before age 8 in girls and 9 in boys). This condition may be treated with <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=306500&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000306500&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3841gonadotropin-releasing hormone (GnRH) agonist</a>

3842 therapy to delay puberty and help the child's growth. <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45498&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045498&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3843Hydrocephalus</a>

3844 may also increase the risk of this late effect. </p>

3845<p id="_933" tabindex="-1">

3846Childhood cancer survivors who were treated with higher doses of radiation to the brain may have low levels of luteinizing hormone or follicle-stimulating hormone. This condition may be treated with sex hormone replacement therapy. The dose will depend on the child's age and whether the child has reached puberty.</p>

3847</li>

3848<li>

3849<strong>

3850Central <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=683346&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000683346&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3851diabetes insipidus</a>

3852</strong>

3853: Central diabetes insipidus may be caused by the absence of or low amounts of all of the hormones made in the front part of the pituitary gland and released into the blood. It may occur in childhood cancer survivors treated with surgery in the area of the hypothalamus or pituitary gland. Signs and symptoms of central diabetes insipidus may include the following:<div class="pdq-content-list">

3854<ul id="_954">

3855<li>

3856Producing large amounts of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46642&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046642&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3857urine</a>

3858.</li>

3859<li>

3860Feeling very thirsty.</li>

3861<li>

3862<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=321374&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000321374&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3863Fatigue</a>

3864.</li>

3865<li>

3866Slowed growth and development.</li>

3867<li>

3868Weight loss

3869for no known reason.</li>

3870</ul>

3871</div>

3872</li>

3873</ul>

3874</div>

3876<section id="_724">

3877<h4 id="_725" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3878Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the neuroendocrine system.</h4>

3879<p id="_1008" tabindex="-1">

3880In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family health history and doing a physical exam, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

3881<div class="pdq-content-list">

3882<ul id="_727">

3883<li>

3884<strong>

3885<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=304685&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000304685&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3886Blood chemistry study</a>

3887</strong>

3888: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain substances, such as <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44033&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044033&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3889glucose</a>

3890, released into the blood by organs and tissues in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance can be a sign of disease.</li>

3891<li>

3892<strong>

3893Blood hormone studies</strong>

3894: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain hormones released into the blood by organs and tissues in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance can be a sign of disease in the organ or tissue that makes it. The blood may be checked for abnormal levels of follicle-stimulating hormone, luteinizing hormone, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=305990&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000305990&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3895estradiol</a>

3896, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45581&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045581&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3897testosterone</a>

3898, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=597113&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000597113&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3899cortisol</a>

3900, or free thyroxine (T4).</li>

3901<li>

3902<strong>

3903<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46068&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046068&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3904Lipid</a>

3905 profile studies</strong>

3906: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of triglycerides, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=407756&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000407756&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3907cholesterol</a>

3908, and low- and high-density lipoprotein cholesterol

3909

3910in the blood.</li>

3911</ul>

3912</div>

3913<p id="_794" tabindex="-1">

3914Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of neuroendocrine late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

3915

3916</p>

3917</section>

3920<h3 id="_878" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3921Testicles and ovaries</h3>

3922<p id="_879" tabindex="-1">

3923For information about late effects in the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46611&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046611&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3924testicles</a>

3925 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46687&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046687&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3931<section id="_847">

3932<h3 id="_848" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3933Metabolic syndrome</h3>

3934<section id="_849">

3935<h4 id="_850" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3936Metabolic syndrome is more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</h4>

3937<p id="_851" tabindex="-1">

3938<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=643126&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000643126&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3939Metabolic syndrome</a>

3940 is a group of medical conditions that includes having too much fat around the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45070&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045070&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3941abdomen</a>

3942 and at least two of the following:</p>

3943<div class="pdq-content-list">

3944<ul id="_852">

3945<li>

3946<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=458091&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000458091&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3947High blood pressure</a>

3948.</li>

3949<li>

3950High levels of triglycerides and low levels of high-density lipoprotein (HDL) cholesterol in the blood.</li>

3951<li>

3952High levels of glucose (sugar) in the blood.</li>

3953</ul>

3954</div>

3955<p id="_853" tabindex="-1">

3956Treatment for these and other childhood cancers may cause metabolic syndrome to occur later in life:</p>

3957<div class="pdq-content-list">

3958<ul id="_854">

3959<li>

3960Acute lymphoblastic leukemia (ALL).</li>

3961<li>

3962Cancers treated with a stem cell transplant.</li>

3963<li>

3964Cancers treated with radiation to the abdomen, such as Wilms tumor or neuroblastoma.</li>

3965</ul>

3966</div>

3967</section>

3968<section id="_855">

3969<h4 id="_856" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3970Radiation therapy increases the risk of metabolic syndrome.</h4>

3971<p id="_962" tabindex="-1">

3972The risk of metabolic syndrome may be increased in childhood cancer survivors after treatment with any of the following:</p>

3973<div class="pdq-content-list">

3974<ul id="_963">

3975<li>

3976Radiation therapy to the brain, abdomen, or pelvis.</li>

3977<li>

3978Total-body irradiation (TBI) as part of a stem cell transplant.</li>

3979<li>

3980<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3981Chemotherapy</a>

3982, such as <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45589&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045589&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

3983alkylating agents</a>

3984.</li>

3985<li>

3986Older age.</li>

3987</ul>

3988</div>

3989</section>

3990<section id="_946">

3991<h4 id="_947" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

3992Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose metabolic syndrome.</h4>

3993<p id="_1009" tabindex="-1">

3994In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family health history and doing a physical exam, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

3995<div class="pdq-content-list">

3996<ul id="_949">

3997<li>

3998<strong>

3999Blood chemistry studies</strong>

4000: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain substances, such as glucose, released into the blood by organs and tissues in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance can be a sign of disease.</li>

4001<li>

4002<strong>

4003Lipid profile studies</strong>

4004: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of triglycerides, cholesterol, and low- and high-density lipoprotein cholesterol

4005

4006in the blood.</li>

4007</ul>

4008</div>

4009<p id="_950" tabindex="-1">

4010Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of metabolic syndrome. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.</p>

4011</section>

4012<section id="_857">

4013<h4 id="_858" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4014Metabolic syndrome may cause heart and blood vessel disease and diabetes.</h4>

4015<p id="_859" tabindex="-1">

4016Metabolic syndrome is linked to an increased risk of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=748138&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000748138&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4017heart and blood vessel disease</a>

4018 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44911&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044911&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4019diabetes</a>

4020. Health habits that decrease these risks include:</p>

4021<div class="pdq-content-list">

4022<ul id="_951">

4023<li>

4024Having a healthy weight.</li>

4025<li>

4026Eating a heart-healthy diet.</li>

4027<li>

4028Having regular exercise.</li>

4029<li>

4030Not smoking.</li>

4031</ul>

4032</div>

4033</section>

4034</section>

4035<section id="_885">

4036<h3 id="_886" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4037Weight</h3>

4038<section id="_248">

4039<h4 id="_249" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4040Being underweight, being overweight, or having obesity is a late effect that is more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.

4041

4042</h4>

4043<p id="_250" tabindex="-1">

4044Treatment for these and other childhood cancers may cause a change in weight:</p>

4045<div class="pdq-content-list">

4046<ul id="_251">

4047<li>

4048Acute lymphoblastic leukemia (ALL).</li>

4049<li>

4050Brain tumors, especially <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46131&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046131&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4051craniopharyngiomas</a>

4052.</li>

4053<li>

4054Cancers treated with radiation to the brain, including TBI as part of a stem cell transplant.</li>

4055</ul>

4056</div>

4057<p id="_982" tabindex="-1">

4058<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45703&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045703&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4059Graft-versus-host disease</a>

4060 may also cause a change in weight for patients treated with a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46695&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046695&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4061stem cell transplant</a>

4062.</p>

4064<section id="_244">

4079anthracyclines</a>

4080).</li>

4081</ul>

4083<p id="_246" tabindex="-1">

4103<li>

4104Being female.</li>

4105<li>

4106Having growth hormone deficiency or low levels of the hormone <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=766473&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000766473&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4107leptin</a>

4108.</li>

4109<li>

4110Not doing enough physical activity to stay at a healthy body weight.</li>

4117</ul>

4163 <h2>

4164Immune System</h2>

4165

4166 <div id="_section_211" class="pdq-sections">

4167<div class="key-points">

4168<h3 id="_211_kpBoxHdr" do-not-show="toc">

4169Key Points</h3>

4170<div id="_kp_section_211_7">

4171<ul>

4172<li>

4173Surgery to remove the spleen increases the risk of immune system late effects.</li>

4174<li>

4175Late effects that affect the immune system may cause infection.</li>

4176<li>

4177Children who have had their spleen removed may need antibiotics to lessen the risk of infection.</li>

4179</div>

4180</div>

4181<section id="_660">

4182<h3 id="_661" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4183Surgery to remove the spleen increases the risk of immune system late effects.</h3>

4184<p id="_662" tabindex="-1">

4185The risk of health problems that affect the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46356&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046356&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4194Surgery</a>

4195 to remove the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46593&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046593&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4200High-dose radiation</a>

4201 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44737&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044737&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4213<section id="_664">

4214<h3 id="_665" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4215Late effects that affect the immune system may cause infection.</h3>

4216<p id="_666" tabindex="-1">

4217<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=390292&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000390292&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4218Late effects</a>

4219 that affect the immune system may increase the risk of very serious <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44123&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044123&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4220bacterial</a>

4221 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45364&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045364&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4222infections</a>

4223. This risk is higher in younger children than in older children and may be greater in the early years after the spleen stops working or is removed by surgery. These <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4224signs</a>

4225 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4226symptoms</a>

4227 may be caused by infection:

4228

4229</p>

4230<div class="pdq-content-list">

4231<ul id="_667">

4232<li>

4233Redness, swelling, or warmth of a part of the body.</li>

4234<li>

4235Pain that is in one part of the body, such as the eye, ear, or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=439429&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000439429&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4236throat</a>

4237.</li>

4238<li>

4239<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450108&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450108&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4240Fever</a>

4241.</li>

4242</ul>

4243</div>

4244<p id="_668" tabindex="-1">

4245An infection may cause other symptoms that depend on the part of the body affected. For example, a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270740&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270740&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4246lung</a>

4247 infection may cause a cough and trouble breathing.</p>

4248</section>

4249<section id="_670">

4250<h3 id="_671" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4251Children who have had their spleen removed may need antibiotics to lessen the risk of infection.</h3>

4252<p id="_919" tabindex="-1">

4253Daily <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45967&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045967&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4254antibiotics</a>

4255 may be prescribed for children younger than 5 whose spleen is no longer working or for at least 1 year after surgery to remove the spleen. For certain high-risk patients, daily antibiotics may be <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44711&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044711&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4256prescribed</a>

4257 throughout childhood and into adulthood. </p>

4258<p id="_673" tabindex="-1">

4259In addition, children with an increased risk of infection should be <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44841&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044841&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4260vaccinated</a>

4261 on a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=346524&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000346524&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4262schedule</a>

4263 through adolescence against the following:</p>

4264<div class="pdq-content-list">

4265<ul id="_674">

4266<li>

4267Pneumococcal disease.</li>

4268<li>

4269Meningococcal disease.</li>

4270<li>

4271<em>

4272Haemophilus influenzae</em>

4273 type b (Hib) disease.</li>

4274<li>

4275Diphtheria-tetanus-pertussis (DTaP).</li>

4276<li>

4277<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46146&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046146&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4278Hepatitis B</a>

4279.</li>

4280</ul>

4281</div>

4282<p id="_864" tabindex="-1">

4283Talk to your child's doctor about whether other childhood <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45937&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045937&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4285 given before cancer treatment need to be repeated.</p>

4295 <h2>

4296Musculoskeletal System</h2>

4297

4298 <div id="_section_459" class="pdq-sections">

4299<div class="key-points">

4300<h3 id="_459_kpBoxHdr" do-not-show="toc">

4301Key Points</h3>

4302<div id="_kp_section_459_8">

4303<ul>

4304<li>

4305Bone and joint late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

4306<li>

4307Radiation therapy, surgery, chemotherapy, and other treatments increase the risk of bone and joint late effects.<ul>

4308<li>

4309Radiation therapy</li>

4310<li>

4311Surgery</li>

4313Chemotherapy and other drug therapy</li>

4317</li>

4320<li>

4321Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the bone and joint.</li>

4322</ul>

4323</div>

4324</div>

4325<section id="_675">

4326<h3 id="_676" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4327Bone and joint late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</h3>

4328<p id="_677" tabindex="-1">

4405<section id="_679">

4406<h3 id="_680" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4407Radiation therapy, surgery, chemotherapy, and other treatments increase the risk of bone and joint late effects.</h3>

4408<section id="_697">

4409<h4 id="_698" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4410Radiation therapy</h4>

4411<p id="_699" tabindex="-1">

4412<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44971&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044971&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4413Radiation therapy</a>

4414 can stop or slow the growth of bone and muscle. The type of bone and joint late effect depends on the part of the body that received radiation therapy. Radiation therapy may cause any of the following:</p>

4415<div class="pdq-content-list">

4416<ul id="_700">

4417<li>

4418Changes in the way the face or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=763008&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000763008&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4419skull</a>

4420 form, especially when <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=440106&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000440106&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4421high-dose radiation</a>

4422 with or without <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4423chemotherapy</a>

4424 is given to children before age 5. </li>

4425<li>

4426Short <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=633093&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000633093&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4427stature</a>

4428 (being shorter than normal).</li>

4429<li>

4430<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=723831&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000723831&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4431Scoliosis</a>

4432 (curving of the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=415914&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000415914&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4433spine</a>

4434) or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=723841&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000723841&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4435kyphosis</a>

4436 (rounding of the spine).</li>

4437<li>

4438One arm or leg is shorter than the other arm or leg.</li>

4439<li>

4440<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45371&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045371&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4441Osteoporosis</a>

4442 (weak or thin bones that can break easily). Fractures (broken bones) can occur with high-dose radiation therapy.</li>

4443<li>

4444Osteoradionecrosis (parts of the bone die from a lack of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270735&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270735&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4445blood</a>

4446 flow, usually affecting the jaw).</li>

4447<li>

4448<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=723860&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000723860&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4449Osteochondroma</a>

4450 (a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46079&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046079&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4451benign tumor</a>

4452 of the bone).</li>

4500Chemotherapy and other drug therapy</h4>

4527<h4 id="_712" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4528Stem cell transplant</h4>

4529<p id="_713" tabindex="-1">

4530A stem cell transplant can affect the bone and joints in different ways: </p>

4531<div class="pdq-content-list">

4532<ul id="_714">

4533<li>

4534<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45930&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045930&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4535Total-body irradiation</a>

4536 given as part of a stem cell transplant may affect the body's ability to make <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=538639&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000538639&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4537growth hormone</a>

4538 and cause short stature (being shorter than normal). It may also cause osteoporosis (weak or thin bones that can break easily). <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=723860&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000723860&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4539Osteochondroma</a>

4540 (a benign tumor of the long bones, such as the arm or leg bones) may form.</li>

4541<li>

4542<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45641&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045641&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4543Chronic</a>

4544 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45703&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045703&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4545graft-versus-host disease</a>

4546 may occur after a stem cell transplant and cause <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=458080&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000458080&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4547joint</a>

4548 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=723866&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000723866&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4549contractures</a>

4550 (tightening of the muscles that causes the joint to shorten and become very stiff). It may also cause osteonecrosis (one or more parts of a bone die from a lack of blood flow).</li>

4551</ul>

4555<section id="_687">

4556<h3 id="_688" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4557Possible signs and symptoms of bone and joint late effects include swelling over a bone or bone and joint pain.</h3>

4558<p id="_689" tabindex="-1">

4559These and other <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4560signs</a>

4561 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4562symptoms</a>

4563 may be caused by bone and joint late effects or by other <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4564conditions</a>

4565:</p>

4566<div class="pdq-content-list">

4567<ul id="_690">

4568<li>

4569Swelling over a bone or bony part of the body.</li>

4570<li>

4571Pain in a bone or joint.</li>

4572<li>

4573Redness or warmth over a bone or joint.</li>

4574<li>

4575Joint stiffness or trouble moving normally.</li>

4576<li>

4577A bone that breaks easily or for no known reason.

4578</li>

4579<li>

4580Short stature (being shorter than normal).</li>

4581<li>

4582One side of the body looks higher than the other side or the body tilts to one side.</li>

4583<li>

4584Always sitting or standing in a slouching position or having the appearance of a hunched back.</li>

4585</ul>

4586</div>

4587<p id="_783" tabindex="-1">

4588Talk to your child's doctor if your child has any of these problems.</p>

4589</section>

4590<section id="_691">

4591<h3 id="_692" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4592Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the bone and joint.</h3>

4593<p id="_1011" tabindex="-1">

4594In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4595health history</a>

4596 and doing a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4597physical exam</a>

4598, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

4599<div class="pdq-content-list">

4600<ul id="_694">

4601<li>

4602<strong>

4603<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=562728&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000562728&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4604Bone mineral density scan</a>

4605</strong>

4606: An <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=689578&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000689578&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4607imaging test</a>

4608 that measures <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=407755&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000407755&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4609bone density</a>

4610 (the amount of bone <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45787&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045787&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4611mineral</a>

4612 in a certain amount of bone) by passing <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45944&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045944&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4613x-rays</a>

4614 with two different energy levels through the bone. It is used to diagnose osteoporosis (weak or thin bones that can break easily). Also called BMD scan, DEXA, DEXA scan, dual energy x-ray absorptiometric scan, dual x-ray absorptiometry, and DXA. </li>

4615<li>

4616<strong>

4617X-ray</strong>

4618: An x-ray is a type of energy beam that can go through the body and onto film, making a picture of areas inside the body, such as bones.</li>

4619</ul>

4620</div>

4621<p id="_792" tabindex="-1">

4622Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of bone and joint late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

4623

4624</p>

4632 <section id="_417">

4633

4634 <h2>

4635Reproductive System</h2>

4636

4637 <div id="_section_417" class="pdq-sections">

4638<div class="key-points">

4639<h3 id="_417_kpBoxHdr" do-not-show="toc">

4640Key Points</h3>

4641<div id="_kp_section_417_9">

4642<ul>

4643<li>

4644Testicles<ul>

4645<li>

4646Testicular late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

4647<li>

4648Surgery, radiation therapy, and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of late effects that affect the testicles. </li>

4649<li>

4650Late effects that affect the testicles may cause certain health problems. </li>

4651<li>

4652Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the testicles.</li>

4653</ul>

4654</li>

4655<li>

4656Ovaries<ul>

4657<li>

4658Ovarian late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

4659<li>

4660Radiation therapy to the abdomen and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of ovarian late effects.

4661 </li>

4662<li>

4663Late effects that affect the ovaries may cause certain health problems.

4664</li>

4665<li>

4666Possible signs and symptoms of ovarian late effects include irregular or absent menstrual periods and hot flashes.</li>

4667<li>

4668Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the ovaries.</li>

4669</ul>

4670</li>

4671<li>

4672Fertility and reproduction<ul>

4673<li>

4674Treatment for cancer may cause infertility in childhood cancer survivors. </li>

4675<li>

4676Childhood cancer survivors may have late effects that affect pregnancy. </li>

4677<li>

4678There are methods that may be used to help childhood cancer survivors have children.</li>

4679<li>

4680Children of childhood cancer survivors are not affected by the parent&#8217;s previous treatment for cancer.</li>

4681</ul>

4682</li>

4683</ul>

4684</div>

4685</div>

4868<h4 id="_735" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4869Ovarian late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</h4>

4870<p id="_736" tabindex="-1">

4871Treatment for these and other childhood cancers may cause <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44984&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044984&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4872ovarian</a>

4873 late effects:</p>

4874<div class="pdq-content-list">

4875<ul id="_737">

4876<li>

4877Acute lymphoblastic leukemia (ALL).</li>

4878<li>

4879Germ cell tumors.</li>

4880<li>

4881Hodgkin lymphoma.</li>

4882<li>

4883<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45946&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045946&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4884Wilms tumor</a>

4885.</li>

4886<li>

4887Cancers treated with a stem cell transplant.</li>

4888</ul>

4889</div>

4890</section>

4891<section id="_424">

4892<h4 id="_425" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

4893Radiation therapy to the abdomen and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of ovarian late effects.

4894 </h4>

4895<p id="_426" tabindex="-1">

4896The risk of ovarian late effects may be increased after treatment with any of the following:</p>

4897<div class="pdq-content-list">

4898<ul id="_427">

4899<li>

4900Surgery to remove one or both <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46687&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046687&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4901ovaries</a>

4902.</li>

4903<li>

4904Chemotherapy with alkylating agents, such as cyclophosphamide, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46603&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046603&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4905mechlorethamine</a>

4906, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45230&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045230&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4907cisplatin</a>

4908, ifosfamide, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46017&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046017&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4909lomustine</a>

4910, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45410&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045410&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4911busulfan</a>

4912, and especially procarbazine.</li>

4913<li>

4914Radiation therapy to the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45070&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045070&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4915abdomen</a>

4916, pelvis, or lower back. In <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450125&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450125&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4917survivors</a>

4918 who had radiation to the abdomen, the damage to the ovaries depends on the radiation dose, age at the time of treatment, and whether all or part of the abdomen received radiation.</li>

4919<li>

4920Radiation therapy to the abdomen or pelvis together with alkylating agents.</li>

4921<li>

4922Radiation therapy to the area near the hypothalamus in the brain.</li>

4923<li>

4924Total-body irradiation before a stem cell transplant. </li>

4925</ul>

4926</div>

4927</section>

4928<section id="_420">

4939, especially in women who had their ovaries removed or were treated with both an <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45589&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045589&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

4941 and radiation therapy to the abdomen.</li>

5002<section id="_987">

5003<h4 id="_988" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5004Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the ovaries.</h4>

5005<p id="_1013" tabindex="-1">

5006In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family health history and doing a physical exam, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following test.</p>

5007<div class="pdq-content-list">

5008<ul id="_990">

5009<li>

5010<strong>

5011Blood hormone studies</strong>

5012: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain hormones released into the blood by organs and tissues in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance can be a sign of disease in the organ or tissue that makes it. The blood may be checked for abnormal levels of follicle-stimulating hormone, luteinizing hormone, or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=305990&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000305990&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5013estradiol</a>

5014.</li>

5015</ul>

5016</div>

5017</section>

5018</section>

5019<section id="_299">

5020<h3 id="_300" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5021Fertility and reproduction</h3>

5022<section id="_743">

5023<h4 id="_744" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5024Treatment for cancer may cause infertility in childhood cancer survivors. </h4>

5025<p id="_745" tabindex="-1">

5026The risk of infertility increases after treatment with the following:</p>

5027<div class="pdq-content-list">

5028<ul id="_746">

5029<li>

5030In boys, treatment with radiation therapy to the testicles.</li>

5031<li>

5032In girls, treatment with radiation therapy to the pelvis, including the ovaries and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46645&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046645&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5033uterus</a>

5034.</li>

5035<li>

5036Radiation therapy to an area near the hypothalamus in the brain or lower back.</li>

5037<li>

5038Total-body irradiation before a stem cell transplant.</li>

5039<li>

5040Chemotherapy with alkylating agents, such as cisplatin, cyclophosphamide, busulfan, lomustine, and procarbazine.</li>

5041<li>

5042Surgery, such as the removal of a testicle or an ovary or lymph nodes in the abdomen.</li>

5043</ul>

5044</div>

5045</section>

5046<section id="_301">

5047<h4 id="_302" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5048Childhood cancer survivors may have late effects that affect pregnancy. </h4>

5049<p id="_303" tabindex="-1">

5050Late effects on <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=666677&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000666677&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5051pregnancy</a>

5052 include increased risk of the following:</p>

5053<div class="pdq-content-list">

5054<ul id="_304">

5055<li>

5056<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=458091&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000458091&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5057High blood pressure</a>

5058.</li>

5059<li>

5060<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44911&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044911&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5061Diabetes</a>

5062 during pregnancy.</li>

5063<li>

5064<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45360&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045360&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5065Anemia</a>

5066.</li>

5067<li>

5068Miscarriage or stillbirth.</li>

5069<li>

5070Low birth-weight babies.</li>

5071<li>

5072Early labor and/or delivery.</li>

5073<li>

5074Delivery by Cesarean section.</li>

5075<li>

5076The <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46400&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046400&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5077fetus</a>

5078 is not in the right position for birth (for example, the foot or buttock is in position to come out before the head).</li>

5079</ul>

5080</div>

5081<p id="_973" tabindex="-1">

5082Some studies have not shown an increased risk of late effects on pregnancy.</p>

5083</section>

5084<section id="_309">

5085<h4 id="_310" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5086There are methods that may be used to help childhood cancer survivors have children.</h4>

5087<p id="_311" tabindex="-1">

5088The following methods may be used so that childhood cancer survivors can have children: </p>

5089<div class="pdq-content-list">

5090<ul id="_312">

5091<li>

5092Freezing the eggs or sperm before cancer treatment in patients who have reached puberty.</li>

5093<li>

5094<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=780385&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000780385&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5095Ovarian transposition</a>

5096 (preventing damage to the ovaries before radiation therapy by moving one or both ovaries and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45687&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045687&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5097fallopian tubes</a>

5098 out of the field of radiation and attaching them to the wall of the abdomen).</li>

5099<li>

5100Testicular sperm extraction (the removal of a small amount of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46683&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046683&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5101tissue</a>

5102 containing sperm from the testicle).</li>

5103<li>

5104Intracytoplasmic sperm <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44678&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044678&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5105injection</a>

5106 (an egg is fertilized with one sperm that is injected into the egg outside the body).</li>

5107<li>

5108

5109<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=440108&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000440108&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5110In vitro fertilization</a>

5111 (IVF) (eggs and sperm are placed together in a container, giving the sperm the chance to enter an egg).

5112</li>

5113</ul>

5114</div>

5115</section>

5116<section id="_314">

5117<h4 id="_315" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5118Children of childhood cancer survivors are not affected by the parent&#8217;s previous treatment for cancer.</h4>

5119<p id="_952" tabindex="-1">

5120The children of childhood cancer survivors do not appear to have an increased risk of birth defects, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46391&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046391&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5121genetic</a>

5122 disease, or cancer.</p>

5123</section>

5133 <h2>

5134Respiratory System</h2>

5135

5136 <div id="_section_318" class="pdq-sections">

5137<div class="key-points">

5138<h3 id="_318_kpBoxHdr" do-not-show="toc">

5139Key Points</h3>

5140<div id="_kp_section_318_10">

5141<ul>

5142<li>

5143Lung late effects are more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.

5144</li>

5145<li>

5146Certain types of chemotherapy and radiation to the lungs increase the risk of lung late effects.

5147</li>

5148<li>

5149Late effects that affect the lungs may cause certain health problems.</li>

5150<li>

5151Possible signs and symptoms of lung late effects include trouble breathing and cough.</li>

5152<li>

5153Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the lung.</li>

5154<li>

5155Health habits that promote healthy lungs are important for survivors of childhood cancer.</li>

5156</ul>

5157</div>

5158</div>

5190<section id="_323">

5191<h3 id="_324" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5192Certain types of chemotherapy and radiation to the lungs increase the risk of lung late effects.

5194<p id="_327" tabindex="-1">

5195The risk of health problems that affect the lungs increases after treatment with the following:

5196

5197</p>

5198<div class="pdq-content-list">

5199<ul id="_328">

5200<li>

5203 to remove all or part of the lung or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44996&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044996&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5206<li>

5207<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5208Chemotherapy</a>

5209. In <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450125&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450125&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5221 to the chest, there is a high risk of lung damage.</li>

5343<section id="_753">

5344<h3 id="_754" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5345Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the lung.</h3>

5346<p id="_1014" tabindex="-1">

5347In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5348health history</a>

5350physical exam</a>

5354<li>

5357Chest x-ray</a>

5358</strong>

5359: An <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45944&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045944&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5362organs</a>

5363 and bones inside the chest. An x-ray is a type of energy beam that can go through the body and onto film, making a picture of areas inside the body.</li>

5364<li>

5365<strong>

5366<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=658018&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000658018&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5369: A test to see how well the lungs are working. It measures how much air the lungs can hold and how quickly air moves into and out of the lungs. 5370oxygen</a>

5371 is used and how much <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=538147&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000538147&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5372carbon dioxide</a>

5373 is given off during breathing. This is also called <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=658017&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000658017&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5374lung function test</a>

5375.

5376</li>

5409

5410 <h2>

5411Senses</h2>

5412

5413 <div id="_section_333" class="pdq-sections">

5414<div class="key-points">

5415<h3 id="_333_kpBoxHdr" do-not-show="toc">

5416Key Points</h3>

5417<div id="_kp_section_333_11">

5418<ul>

5419<li>

5420Hearing<ul>

5421<li>

5422Hearing problems are a late effect that is more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

5423<li>

5424Radiation therapy to the brain and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of hearing loss. </li>

5425<li>

5426Hearing loss is the most common sign of hearing late effects.</li>

5427<li>

5428Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the ear and hearing problems.</li>

5429</ul>

5430</li>

5431<li>

5432Seeing<ul>

5433<li>

5434Eye and vision problems are a late effect that is more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

5435<li>

5436Radiation therapy to the brain or head increases the risk of eye problems or vision loss.</li>

5437<li>

5438Late effects that affect the eye may cause certain health problems.</li>

5439<li>

5440Possible signs and symptoms of eye and vision late effects include changes in vision and dry eyes.</li>

5441<li>

5442Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the eye and vision problems.</li>

5443</ul>

5444</li>

5445</ul>

5446</div>

5447</div>

5492Soft tissue sarcoma</a>

5493.</li>

5494<li>
