5501<section id="_338">

5502<h4 id="_339" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5503Radiation therapy to the brain and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of hearing loss. </h4>

5504<p id="_340" tabindex="-1">

5505The risk of hearing loss is increased in childhood cancer <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=450125&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000450125&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5506survivors</a>

5507 after treatment with the following:

5508

5509</p>

5510<div class="pdq-content-list">

5511<ul id="_341">

5512<li>

5513Certain types of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045214&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5514chemotherapy</a>

5515, such as <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45230&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045230&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5516cisplatin</a>

5517 or high-<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44664&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044664&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5518dose</a>

5519 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45182&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045182&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5525 to the brain.

5530The risk of hearing loss is greater in childhood cancer survivors who were young at the time of treatment (the younger the child, the greater the risk), were treated for a brain tumor, or received radiation therapy to the brain and chemotherapy at the same time.</p>

5532<section id="_757">

5533<h4 id="_758" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5534Hearing loss is the most common sign of hearing late effects.</h4>

5535<p id="_759" tabindex="-1">

5536These and other <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000750109&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5537signs</a>

5538 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045022&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5539symptoms</a>

5540 may be caused by hearing late effects or by other <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000651193&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5541conditions</a>

5542:

5543

5544</p>

5545<div class="pdq-content-list">

5546<ul id="_760">

5547<li>

5548Hearing loss.</li>

5549<li>

5550Ringing in the ears.</li>

5551<li>

5552Feeling dizzy.</li>

5553<li>

5554Too much hardened wax in the ear.</li>

5555</ul>

5556</div>

5557<p id="_761" tabindex="-1">

5558Hearing loss may occur during treatment, soon after treatment ends, or several months or years after treatment ends and worsen over time. Talk to your child's doctor if your child has any of these problems.</p>

5559</section>

5560<section id="_762">

5561<h4 id="_763" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5562Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the ear and hearing problems.</h4>

5563<p id="_1015" tabindex="-1">

5564In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5565health history</a>

5566 and doing a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5567physical exam</a>

5568, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

5569<div class="pdq-content-list">

5570<ul id="_765">

5571<li>

5572<strong>

5573Otoscopic exam</strong>

5574: An exam of the ear. An otoscope is used to look at the ear canal and the eardrum to check for signs of <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45364&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045364&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5575infection</a>

5576 or hearing loss. Sometimes the otoscope has a plastic bulb that is squeezed to release a small puff of air into the ear canal. In a healthy ear, the eardrum will move. If there is <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44669&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044669&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5577fluid</a>

5578 behind the eardrum, it will not move.</li>

5579<li>

5580<strong>

5581Hearing test</strong>

5582: A hearing test can be done in different ways depending on the child's age. The test is done to check if the child can hear soft and loud sounds and low- and high-pitched sounds. Each ear is checked separately. The child may also be asked if he or she can hear the high-pitched hum of a tuning fork when it is placed behind the ear or on the forehead. </li>

5583</ul>

5584</div>

5585<p id="_796" tabindex="-1">

5586Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of hearing late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

5587

5588</p>

5589</section>

5740<section id="_773">

5741<h4 id="_774" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

5742Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the eye and vision problems.</h4>

5743<p id="_1016" tabindex="-1">

5744In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family health history and doing a physical exam, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

5745<div class="pdq-content-list">

5746<ul id="_776">

5747<li>

5748<strong>

5749Eye exam with <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=257207&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000257207&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5750dilated</a>

5751 <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=546600&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000546600&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5752pupil</a>

5753</strong>

5754: An exam of the eye in which the pupil is dilated (widened) with medicated eye drops to allow the doctor to look through the <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=572035&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000572035&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5755lens</a>

5756 and pupil to the retina. The inside of the eye, including the retina and the optic nerve, is checked using an instrument that makes a narrow beam of light. This is sometimes called a slit-lamp exam. If there is a tumor, the doctor may take pictures over time to keep track of changes in the size of the tumor and how fast it is growing.

5757</li>

5758<li>

5759<strong>

5760<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=534231&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000534231&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

5761Indirect ophthalmoscopy</a>

5762</strong>

5763: An exam of the inside of the back of the eye using a small magnifying lens and a light.

5764</li>

5765</ul>

5766</div>

5767<p id="_797" tabindex="-1">

5768Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of eye and vision late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

5781 <h2>

5782Urinary System</h2>

5783

5784 <div id="_section_363" class="pdq-sections">

5785<div class="key-points">

5786<h3 id="_363_kpBoxHdr" do-not-show="toc">

5787Key Points</h3>

5788<div id="_kp_section_363_12">

5789<ul>

5790<li>

5791Kidney<ul>

5792<li>

5793Kidney problems are a late effect that is more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

5794<li>

5795Certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of kidney late effects.</li>

5796<li>

5797Late effects that affect the kidney may cause certain health problems.</li>

5798<li>

5799Possible signs and symptoms of kidney late effects include problems urinating and swelling of the feet or hands.</li>

5800<li>

5801Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the kidney.</li>

5802<li>

5803Health habits that promote healthy kidneys are important for survivors of childhood cancer.</li>

5804</ul>

5805</li>

5806<li>

5807Bladder<ul>

5808<li>

5809Bladder problems are a late effect that is more likely to occur after treatment for certain childhood cancers.</li>

5810<li>

5811Surgery to the pelvic area and certain types of chemotherapy increase the risk of bladder late effects.</li>

5812<li>

5813Late effects that affect the bladder may cause certain health problems.</li>

5814<li>

5815Possible signs and symptoms of bladder late effects include changes in urination and swelling of the feet or hands.</li>

5816<li>

5817Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the bladder.</li>

5818</ul>

5819</li>

5820</ul>

6000<section id="_810">

6001<h4 id="_811" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

6002Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the kidney.</h4>

6003<p id="_1017" tabindex="-1">

6004In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000798522&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6005health history</a>

6006 and doing a <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000270871&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6007physical exam</a>

6008, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

6009<div class="pdq-content-list">

6010<ul id="_813">

6011<li>

6012<strong>

6013<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=304685&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000304685&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6014Blood chemistry study</a>

6015</strong>

6016: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain substances, such as magnesium, calcium, and potassium, released into the blood by <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=257523&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000257523&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6017organs</a>

6018 and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46683&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046683&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6019tissues</a>

6020 in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance may be a sign of kidney disease.

6021</li>

6022<li>

6023<strong>

6024<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46641&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046641&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6025Urinalysis</a>

6026</strong>

6027: A test to check the color of urine and its contents, such as sugar, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46092&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046092&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6028protein</a>

6029, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046124&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6030red blood cells</a>

6031, and <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45993&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045993&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6032white blood cells</a>

6033.</li>

6034<li>

6035<strong>

6036<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46157&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046157&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6037Ultrasound</a>

6038 exam</strong>

6039: A procedure in which high-energy sound waves (ultrasound) are bounced off internal tissues or organs, such as the kidney, and make echoes. The echoes form a picture of body tissues called a sonogram. The picture can be printed to be looked at later.</li>

6040</ul>

6041</div>

6042<p id="_815" tabindex="-1">

6043Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of kidney late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.

6048<h4 id="_817" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

6049Health habits that promote healthy kidneys are important for survivors of childhood cancer.</h4>

6050<p id="_818" tabindex="-1">

6052<div class="pdq-content-list">

6055Whether it is safe to play sports that have a high risk of heavy contact or impact such as football or hockey. </li>

6056<li>

6057Bicycle safety and avoiding handlebar injuries.</li>

6058<li>

6059Wearing a seatbelt around the hips, not the waist.</li>

6060</ul>

6115<section id="_404">

6116<h4 id="_405" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

6117Late effects that affect the bladder may cause certain health problems.</h4>

6118<p id="_406" tabindex="-1">

6119Bladder late effects and related health problems include the following:</p>

6120<div class="pdq-content-list">

6127 of the inside of the bladder wall, which leads to bleeding).</li>

6129Thickening of the bladder wall.</li>

6130<li>

6131Decreased <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46642&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046642&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6132urine</a>

6133 storage.</li>

6134<li>

6135Trouble emptying the bladder.</li>

6136<li>

6137<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46354&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046354&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6138Incontinence</a>

6139.</li>

6140<li>

6141A blockage in the kidney, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46638&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046638&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6142ureter</a>

6143, bladder, or <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=46640&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000046640&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6144urethra</a>

6145.</li>

6146<li>

6147Urinary tract <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45364&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045364&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6148infection</a>

6149 (<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=45641&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000045641&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6150chronic</a>

6151).</li>

6152</ul>

6153</div>

6154</section>

6155<section id="_820">

6156<h4 id="_821" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

6157Possible signs and symptoms of bladder late effects include changes in urination and swelling of the feet or hands.</h4>

6158<p id="_822" tabindex="-1">

6159These and other signs and symptoms may be caused by bladder late effects or by other conditions:

6160

6161</p>

6162<div class="pdq-content-list">

6163<ul id="_823">

6164<li>

6165Feeling the need to urinate without being able to do so.</li>

6166<li>

6167Frequent urination (especially at night).</li>

6168<li>

6169Trouble urinating.</li>

6170<li>

6171Feeling like the bladder does not empty completely after urination.</li>

6172<li>

6173Swelling of the legs, ankles, feet, face, or hands.</li>

6174<li>

6175Little or no bladder control.</li>

6176<li>

6177Blood in the urine.</li>

6178</ul>

6179</div>

6180<p id="_824" tabindex="-1">

6181Talk to your child's doctor if your child has any of these problems.</p>

6182</section>

6183<section id="_825">

6184<h4 id="_826" type="keypoint" do-not-show="toc">

6185Certain tests and procedures are used to diagnose health problems in the bladder.</h4>

6186<p id="_1018" tabindex="-1">

6187In addition to asking about your child&#8217;s personal and family health history and doing a physical exam, your child&#8217;s doctor may perform the following tests and procedures.</p>

6188<div class="pdq-content-list">

6189<ul id="_828">

6190<li>

6191<strong>

6192Blood chemistry study</strong>

6193: A procedure in which a blood sample is checked to measure the amounts of certain substances, such as magnesium, calcium, and potassium, released into the blood by organs and tissues in the body. An unusual (higher or lower than normal) amount of a substance may be a sign of bladder problems.</li>

6194<li>

6195<strong>

6196Urinalysis</strong>

6197: A test to check the color of urine and its contents, such as sugar, protein, red blood cells, and white blood cells.</li>

6198<li>

6199<strong>

6200<a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=750105&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000750105&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6201Urine culture</a>

6202</strong>

6203: A test to check for <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44123&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044123&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6204bacteria</a>

6205, <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=770605&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000770605&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6206yeast</a>

6207, or other <a class="definition" type="GlossaryTermRefs" href="/Common/PopUps/popDefinition.aspx?id=44059&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov" onclick="javascript:popWindow('defbyid','CDR0000044059&amp;version=patient&amp;language=English&amp;dictionary=Cancer.gov'); return(false);">

6208microorganisms</a>

6209 in the urine when there are symptoms of infection. Urine cultures can help identify the type of microorganism that is causing an infection. Treatment of the infection depends on the type of microorganism that is causing the infection.</li>

6210<li>

6211<strong>

6212Ultrasound exam</strong>

6213: A procedure in which high-energy sound waves (ultrasound) are bounced off internal tissues or organs, such as the bladder, and make echoes. The echoes form a picture of body tissues called a sonogram. The picture can be printed to be looked at later.</li>

6214</ul>

6215</div>

6216<p id="_831" tabindex="-1">

6217Talk to your child's doctor about whether your child needs to have tests and procedures to check for signs of bladder late effects. If tests are needed, find out how often they should be done.</p>

6218</section>

6219</section>

6220</div>

6221

6222 </section>

6223

6305 <section id="_AboutThis_1">

6306

6307 <h2>

6308About This PDQ Summary</h2>

6309

6310 <div id="_section_AboutThis_1" class="pdq-sections">

6311<section id="_AboutThis_2">

6312<h3 id="_AboutThis_2_toc">

6313About PDQ</h3>

6314<p id="_AboutThis_3" tabindex="-1">

6315Physician Data Query (PDQ) is the National Cancer Institute's (NCI's) comprehensive cancer information database. The PDQ database contains summaries of the latest published information on cancer prevention, detection, genetics, treatment, supportive care, and complementary and alternative medicine. Most summaries come in two versions. The health professional versions have detailed information written in technical language. The patient versions are written in easy-to-understand, nontechnical language. Both versions have cancer information that is accurate and up to date and most versions are also available in <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/espanol/publicaciones/pdq" title="https://www.cancer.gov/espanol/publicaciones/pdq">

6316Spanish</a>

6317.</p>

6318<p id="_AboutThis_4" tabindex="-1">

6319PDQ is a service of the NCI. The NCI is part of the National Institutes of Health (NIH). NIH is the federal government&#8217;s center of biomedical research. The PDQ summaries are based on an independent review of the medical literature. They are not policy statements of the NCI or the NIH.</p>

6320</section>

6321<section id="_AboutThis_5">

6322<h3 id="_AboutThis_5_toc">

6323Purpose of This Summary</h3>

6324<p id="_AboutThis_6" tabindex="-1">

6325This PDQ cancer information summary has current information about the late effects of treatment for childhood cancer. It is meant to inform and help patients, families, and caregivers. It does not give formal guidelines or recommendations for making decisions about health care.</p>

6326</section>

6327<section id="_AboutThis_7">

6328<h3 id="_AboutThis_7_toc">

6329Reviewers and Updates</h3>

6330<p id="_AboutThis_8" tabindex="-1">

6331Editorial Boards write the PDQ cancer information summaries and keep them up to date. These Boards are made up of experts in cancer treatment and other specialties related to cancer. The summaries are reviewed regularly and changes are made when there is new information. The date on each summary ("Updated") is the date of the most recent change.

6332</p>

6333<p id="_AboutThis_9" tabindex="-1">

6334The information in this patient summary was taken from the health professional version, which is reviewed regularly and updated as needed, by the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq/editorial-boards/pediatric-treatment" title="https://www.cancer.gov/publications/pdq/editorial-boards/pediatric-treatment">

6335PDQ Pediatric Treatment Editorial Board</a>

6336.

6337</p>

6338</section>

6339<section id="_AboutThis_10">

6340<h3 id="_AboutThis_10_toc">

6341Clinical Trial Information</h3>

6342<p id="_AboutThis_11" tabindex="-1">

6343A clinical trial is a study to answer a scientific question, such as whether one treatment is better than another. Trials are based on past studies and what has been learned in the laboratory. Each trial answers certain scientific questions in order to find new and better ways to help cancer patients. During treatment clinical trials, information is collected about the effects of a new treatment and how well it works. If a clinical trial shows that a new treatment is better than one currently being used, the new treatment may become "standard." Patients may want to think about taking part in a clinical trial. Some clinical trials are open only to patients who have not started treatment.

6344</p>

6345<p id="_AboutThis_12" tabindex="-1">

6346Clinical trials can be found online at <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials" title="https://www.cancer.gov/about-cancer/treatment/clinical-trials">

6347NCI's website</a>

6348. For more information, call the <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/contact-center" title="https://www.cancer.gov/contact/contact-center">

6349Cancer Information Service</a>

6350 (CIS), NCI's contact center, at 1-800-4-CANCER (1-800-422-6237).

6351</p>

6352</section>

6353<section id="_AboutThis_13">

6354<h3 id="_AboutThis_13_toc">

6355Permission to Use This Summary</h3>

6356<p id="_AboutThis_14" tabindex="-1">

6357PDQ is a registered trademark. The content of PDQ documents can be used freely as text. It cannot be identified as an NCI PDQ cancer information summary unless the whole summary is shown and it is updated regularly. However, a user would be allowed to write a sentence such as &#8220;NCI&#8217;s PDQ cancer information summary about breast cancer prevention states the risks in the following way: [include excerpt from the summary].&#8221;

6358</p>

6359<p id="_AboutThis_15" tabindex="-1">

6360The best way to cite this PDQ summary is:</p>

6361<p id="_AboutThis_21" tabindex="-1">

6362PDQ&#174; Pediatric Treatment Editorial Board. PDQ Late Effects of Treatment for Childhood Cancer. Bethesda, MD: National Cancer Institute. Updated &lt;MM/DD/YYYY&gt;. Available at: <a href="https://www.cancer.gov/types/childhood-cancers/late-effects-pdq" title="https://www.cancer.gov/types/childhood-cancers/late-effects-pdq">

6363https://www.cancer.gov/types/childhood-cancers/late-effects-pdq</a>

6364. Accessed &lt;MM/DD/YYYY&gt;. [PMID: 26389365]</p>

6365<p id="_AboutThis_16" tabindex="-1">

6366Images in this summary are used with permission of the author(s), artist, and/or publisher for use in the PDQ summaries only. If you want to use an image from a PDQ summary and you are not using the whole summary, you must get permission from the owner. It cannot be given by the National Cancer Institute. Information about using the images in this summary, along with many other images related to cancer can be found in <a href="https://visualsonline.cancer.gov/" title="https://visualsonline.cancer.gov/">

6367Visuals Online</a>

6368. Visuals Online is a collection of more than 3,000 scientific images.

6369</p>

6370</section>

6376Managing Cancer Care</a>

6377 page.</p>
